      <p class="description">
        SUSCRIBETE CON PRUEBA GRATUITA SIN COMPROMISO - LA PELUQUERÍA CANINA A TU ALCANCE, TODAS LAS RAZAS TODAS LAS TÉCNICAS.  Solo los canales muy populares pueden financiarse con la publicidad. La Peluquería Canina es un tema minoritario dentro del universo Youtube, por eso hemos buscado esta manera de financiar el canal, te ofrecemos a cambio VÍDEOS EXCLUSIVOS PARA SUSCRIPTORES DE PAGO Y SIN PUBLICIDAD. Con tu aportación mensual contribuyes a financiar nuevos vídeos. cada mes automaticamente Google cargará en tu cuenta la suscripción.

        <h1 class="title-wrap">
          <span class="qualified-channel-title ellipsized has-badge"><span class="qualified-channel-title-wrapper"><span dir="ltr" class="qualified-channel-title-text g-hovercard" data-ytid="UClVPihc-qy7on0hGMsc0_hw" data-name="gb_ch_rec"             ><a dir="ltr" href="/user/EnchantedMob" class=" yt-uix-sessionlink" title="EnchantedMob™" data-sessionlink="ei=vEszV4rIIsK0qQWMyIfABg&amp;feature=gb_ch_rec"      >EnchantedMob™</a></span></span><a href="//support.google.com/youtube/answer/3046484?hl=en" target="_blank" class="qualified-channel-title-badge"><span aria-label="Verified" data-tooltip-text="Verified" class="yt-channel-title-icon-verified yt-uix-tooltip yt-sprite"></span></a></span>
        </h1>
      </div>
      <p class="description">
        I animate Minecraft into popular or random topics! I like to make animated music videos a lot. The program I use is Blender. I also have a Website, Twitter, and Steam Group if you want some of the latest information about upcoming events for my channel. My music videos are focused on Minecraft, but I also animated(ed) FNAF and I also animate Undertale videos!

My main focus on the channel is to create &quot;Minecraft Music Videos&quot;; however, I also try to release short animations every now and then to keep the channel active, while I work on larger projects.

While Animating is a long a time consuming process, I do my best to get at least one short animation every month.
      </p>

          <span class="qualified-channel-title ellipsized has-badge"><span class="qualified-channel-title-wrapper"><span dir="ltr" class="qualified-channel-title-text g-hovercard" data-ytid="UCuJLxDbMKgE_cC-eG0NNttg" data-name="gb_ch_rec"             ><a dir="ltr" href="/channel/UCuJLxDbMKgE_cC-eG0NNttg" class=" yt-uix-sessionlink" title="Drifting - Topic" data-sessionlink="ei=vEszV4rIIsK0qQWMyIfABg&amp;feature=gb_ch_rec"      >Drifting - Topic</a></span></span><span class="qualified-channel-title-badge"><span aria-label="Auto-generated by YouTube" data-tooltip-text="Auto-generated by YouTube" class="yt-channel-title-autogenerated yt-uix-tooltip yt-sprite"></span></span></span>
        </h1>
      </div>
      <p class="description">
        Drifting is a driving technique where the driver intentionally oversteers, causing loss of traction in the rear wheels or all tires, while maintaining control for the entirety of a corner. A car is drifting when the rear slip angle is greater than the front slip angle, to such an extent that often the front wheels are pointing in the opposite direction to the turn.
As a motorsport discipline, professional drifting competitions are held worldwide and are judged according to the speed, angle, showmanship and line taken through a corner or set of corners.
This channel was generated automatically by YouTube&#39;s video discovery system.
      </p>

        <h1 class="title-wrap">
          <span class="qualified-channel-title ellipsized"><span class="qualified-channel-title-wrapper"><span dir="ltr" class="qualified-channel-title-text g-hovercard" data-ytid="UC52X5wxOL_s5yw0dQk7NtgA" data-name="gb_ch_rec"             ><a dir="ltr" href="/user/AssociatedPress" class=" yt-uix-sessionlink" title="Associated Press" data-sessionlink="ei=vEszV4rIIsK0qQWMyIfABg&amp;feature=gb_ch_rec"      >Associated Press</a></span></span></span>
        </h1>
      </div>
      <p class="description">
        The Associated Press is the essential global news network, delivering fast, unbiased news from every corner of the world to all media platforms and formats.

AP&#39;s commitment to independent, comprehensive journalism has deep roots. Founded in 1846, AP has covered all the major news events of the past 165 years, providing high-quality, informed reporting of everything from wars and elections to championship games and royal weddings. AP is the largest and most trusted source of independent news and information.

Today, AP employs the latest technology to collect and distribute content - we have daily uploads covering the latest and breaking news in the world of politics, sport and entertainment. Join us in a conversation about world events, the newsgathering process or whatever aspect of the news universe you find interesting or important.

        <h1 class="title-wrap">
          <span class="qualified-channel-title ellipsized"><span class="qualified-channel-title-wrapper"><span dir="ltr" class="qualified-channel-title-text g-hovercard" data-ytid="UC52X5wxOL_s5yw0dQk7NtgA" data-name="gb_ch_rec"             ><a dir="ltr" href="/user/AssociatedPress" class=" yt-uix-sessionlink" title="Associated Press" data-sessionlink="ei=vEszV4rIIsK0qQWMyIfABg&amp;feature=gb_ch_rec"      >Associated Press</a></span></span></span>
        </h1>
      </div>
      <p class="description">
        The Associated Press is the essential global news network, delivering fast, unbiased news from every corner of the world to all media platforms and formats.

AP&#39;s commitment to independent, comprehensive journalism has deep roots. Founded in 1846, AP has covered all the major news events of the past 165 years, providing high-quality, informed reporting of everything from wars and elections to championship games and royal weddings. AP is the largest and most trusted source of independent news and information.

Today, AP employs the latest technology to collect and distribute content - we have daily uploads covering the latest and breaking news in the world of politics, sport and entertainment. Join us in a conversation about world events, the newsgathering process or whatever aspect of the news universe you find interesting or important.
      </p>
